2) Karloff Lagarde Jr., Mr. Cóndor, Perro Silva b Brillante, Diamante, Zafiro [mask]
## 19:08, *** 1/2. 3 hairs vs 3 masks. Picudo was in the rudos corners, Baby Rose was in the tecnicos corners. Brillante had an injured shoulder. Bloody match. Picudo helped the rudos won the first fall. Lagarde was pinned in the second. Brillante missed a dive on Silva, and all 3 rudos put Zafiro in a submission to win.
3) Fuerza Guerrera, Juventud Guerrera, Psicosis DQ El Hijo Del Santo, Octagón, Rey Misterio Jr.
## 33:32, ****3/4. Fuerza was IWA middleweight champion, Juvi was WWA lightweight champion and Psicosis was WWA welterweight champion. All the titles were on the line, with the rudo taking the fall losing his title. Perro Aguayo Jr. debuted in the tecnico corner, while Santo Negro (who could no longer be called that name) was in the rudo corner. Not Santo Negro fould Santo, and Psicosis leg dropped him for the pin. Juvi attacked Aguayo Jr., Aguayo Jr. came back, rudos beat him donw and kept everyone else out wihle the destroyed Aguayo Jr. Aguayo Sr. made the save.
4) La Parka, Latin Lover, Máscara Sagrada, Volador b Blue Panther, Heavy Metal, Jerry Estrada, Misterioso
## 26:58, *** 1/4. tecnicos took 2/3. First two falls were bad. Misteroso fouled Latin, Volador fouled Misterioso. Voaldor and Misterioso agreed to a mask match, which was to take place in Los Angeles.
5) Cien Caras b Konnan, Perro Aguayo Sr. [Rio Nilo Cup]
## 17:42, *** 1/2. Seconds were Octagon, Mascara Sagrada and Mascara Ano 2000. Konnan was counted out to lose the first fall, Caras pinned Aguayo with a double stomp, Konnan pinned Caras, Aguayo gave Caras a silla to the floor, and Mascara Ano 2000 cracked him in the head with a beer bottle, knocking him out. Konnan busted Caras open, Tirantes looked at the cut to see if the match needed to be stopped, and Mascara 2000 fouled him too. Cien fouled Octagon, Mascara fouled Konnan, Cien fouled Konnan again and Tirantes awoke to count the pin.
&& Originally billed as a TripleMania card, but the name was dropped officially after a related Mexico City card was canceled.

## ****. Tirantes started as ref, but Pena replaced him after one fall with Pepe Casas. Misterioso won the first with a boston crab in 4:10. Blue Panther, seconding Misterioso, attacked Voaldor between falls and Misterioso posted Volador. Panther accidentally hit Misterioso with a chair in the second, and the two fought leading to Misterioso being counted out in the second. Panther attacked Volador in the third and was about to piledriver him when Misterioso broke it up. Volador toped Panther, but Panther got up and knocked out Misterioso on the floor. Volador and Rey Misterio brought Misterioso back in the ring so he wouldn't lose that way. Volador covered Misterioso, but pulled him up at two. Misterioso would not wake up, so Volador put Misterioso on top for the three count and lost his mask, 3:12. Volador was Ramón Ibarra Banda of Monterrey. Misterioso refused to accept the mask and hugged his ex-tag team partner.

## Psicosis and Rey Jr. were seconds, then Perro Jr., Picudo and Jerry Estrada ran in and interfered to cause a DQ. Title changed on DQ, making Perro new champion. (Wasn't planned to be at title change, but the fans were throwing garbage at the ring and the promotion paniced to calm them down.)
5) Canek, Cien Caras, Pentagon, Pierroth Jr. DQ Halcón Dorado Jr., Konnan, La Parka, Octagón
## Canek & Halcon Dorado were mystery partners. The plans had been for Fishman & Ultimo Dragon, but Canek met with Pena and agreed to come in, and Dragon couldn't because CMLL still his working permits. Konnan and Canek had problems during the match, causing Konnan to walk out of the match, though he eventually returned. They argued again later in the lockerroom and both told Pena they didn't want to work together. Canek said he'd work for AAA but not with Konnan, and Konnan wanted Canek gone. In the actual match, all the rudos turned on Cien Caras and Konnan made the save. Cien accepted a handshake but not a hug from Konnan.
